      // BannerlordExpanded.WandererCreator, Version=0.0.1.0, Culture=neutral, PublicKeyToken=null

using System;
using BannerlordExpanded.WandererCreator.Controllers;
using BannerlordExpanded.WandererCreator.UI;
using TaleWorlds.Core;
using TaleWorlds.Engine;
using TaleWorlds.MountAndBlade;
using TaleWorlds.ScreenSystem;

public override void OnLoadFinished()
{
	((MBGameManager)this).OnLoadFinished();
	FileLogger.Log("OnLoadFinished called");
	try
	{
		Utilities.DisableGlobalLoadingWindow();
	}
	catch
	{
	}
	try
	{
		FileLogger.Log("Attempting to force load XMLs...");
		MBObjectManagerExtensions.LoadXML(Game.Current.ObjectManager, "Monsters", false);
		FileLogger.Log("Force loading XMLs completed (trace).");
	}
	catch (Exception ex)
	{
		FileLogger.Log("Warning: Failed to force load XMLs: " + ex.Message);
	}
	Game.Current.GameStateManager.RegisterListener((IGameStateManagerListener)(object)this);
	FileLogger.Log("Registered IGameStateManagerListener");
	Game.Current.GameStateManager.PushState((GameState)(object)Game.Current.GameStateManager.CreateState<CreatorState>(), 0);
	FileLogger.Log("Pushed CreatorState (base GameState)");
	ScreenManager.PushScreen((ScreenBase)(object)new CreatorScreen());
	FileLogger.Log("Pushed CreatorScreen");
	EditorController instance = EditorController.Instance;
	if (instance != null)
	{
		instance.Start();
		FileLogger.Log("Controller Started");
	}
}
